< Review>
Checking city walk out with my boyfriend, we decided to try out Pinks there. First things first, this is not like the original, it was more of a commercial fast food joint. If you've ever had the original, you know their hot dogs have that char and flavor from a grill which this place lacked.

We got the ozzy spicy dog and it was ok. The hot dog didn't taste grilled rather boiled and the toppings were like any other fast food guac and nacho cheese. Overall, this place doesn't compare to the original, probably never coming back to the one at City Walk. Overall, two stars because although it didn't live up to the original it was an ok hot dog.<//Review>

<date>1569679917007< /date><rate>5< /rate><text>This is a gorgeous road. It stretches from Lee Vining to the west on a pass which goes all the way to Yosemite.  There are lakes and creeks and the best time to take photos is during fall or first snow.

The road is very windy and steep so take it slow.  During this time of year (not sure if this is all times) you will be required to stop and pay I believe $35 per car at the 12 mile mark.

The drive however for those 12 miles is worth it.  You can turn around and not pay.

I highly recommend taking this pass if you are up at the Mammoth Lakes area or Mono Lake.

We didn't have much time, so we only took a few photos, but there are so many cool places to check out.  Totally cool drive!</text><Pics>None</Pics><Resp>None</Resp>< gmap_id>

<Gmap_id>0x80c333064079945b:0x91c97e2182f03fd5</Gmap_id><name>Duan Dao (DaoHaus)</name><Review>We found this place last night after we figured out that they took over the space that was once Jollebee's. Looked interesting as it's been a while since we stepped out of our comfort zone and tried fusion *insert national cuisine*. Menu choices are limited so you won't get stuck standing there trying to decide what to have.

My two girls ordered bolgogi rice bowl, I ordered crawfish with spicy Cajun sausages over a bed of pasta with this creamy garlic sauce that you drizzle over and mix it up.

Wife got bulgogi over garlic noodles.

Pricing:  cost per order was setting $10 so it was reasonable considering that you get a decent amount of food.

Covid planning:  they separated the booths to every other one so thankfully we were able to find a spot for our family to sit.

The bulgogi bowl cane with some lettuce, pickled daikon and carrots and some sauce to mix your rice up with the meat. If you've never tried bulgogi you will be in for a treat as it's got the savory and slight sweetness to it that makes you want to eat and eat.

The crawfish Cajun sausage pats with the creamy garlic sauce was pretty damn amazing. Had just the right amount of spice and my son and I dusted our plate in a hot ny minute.

Definitely give them a go since they would really benefit from the place being recently opened before the Covid shutdown.<//Review>< time>

The tops still looked good, but because I wanted them to look their best I opted for the "Ladies Ultra" service. What a huge mistake! The soles are now fine, but the tops came back looking terrible -- strangely dull and monotone! NuShoe's "ultra" service seems to consist of spraying the entire shoe black, including the patent-leather toe, patent silver-metallic strap, and the silver metal rings and buckle. It took me more than an hour (using rubbing alcohol, q-tips, and a microfiber cloth) to carefully remove the black spray from the metal and patent-leather parts. Fortunately, I was largely able to restore the metal and patent-leather parts to their former color and shine. What a disappointment and a waste of $80.</text>

<user>100531252099964496238</user><Gmap_id>0x80d9464af26784b9:0xccafc0ff735fc1b8</Gmap_id>< Text>
About a year ago, during the pandemic, I sent my husband's black wingtips to Nushoe for new soles and heels and an overall refurbishment of the leather uppers, which were very scuffed and scratched. He has had these shoes for probably 30 years, and they were in bad shape. When the repaired shoes arrived, I was amazed because they looked like a brand new pair. The new soles and heels look quite durable, and the shine on the uppers is blinding.

I highly recommend Nushoes. The cost is a little high, but the improvement to my husband's shoes probably means he will not need to buy another pair of dress shoes for the remainder of his life. Customer service was also very helpful when I called for advice on which option to choose before I placed my order and mailed the shoes. The process for shipment between the customer and Nushoes is very convenient, too.</Text>

< Review>
I saw Dr. DiCesare for the removal of a cyst on my right wrist.  He removed the cyst and gave me three stitches and did a biopsy. He told me his office would be in touch regarding the biopsy results and that I should return in two weeks to remove the stitches.  Over that period of time, the area was inflamed and continued to look red.  No word was received on the results of the biopsy.  My attempts to call the office proved futile because the phone number I had was incorrect.  When I got to the office to remove the stitches, the nurse babbled something about not being able to give me the biopsy results because they were "inconclusive."  With Dr. DiCesare away on vacation, no one was able to interpret the results.  One thing was sure, they did not show a definite negative reading.

At the office, I was told that Dr. DiCesare was not going to see me.  The assistant removed the stitches from my still inflamed wrist, placed some kind of steri bandage and provided no further instructions.

I am lucky that my brother is a doctor, and I will send this biopsy report to him to review.

I will under no circumstance recommend this office.  Any doctor who does not have the time to see a patient for follow-up is not worthy of the name.</Review>
